+def _normalize_unicode_minus(text: str) -> str:
+    """I-gen-005 fix: replace unicode minus (U+2212), en-dash (U+2013),
+    em-dash (U+2014), and figure-dash (U+2012) with ASCII '-' so number
+    extraction matches consistently. Evidence text scraped from PDFs /
+    HTML often uses unicode minus (`−1.07`) while LLM output uses ASCII
+    (`-1.07`); raw set comparison previously failed for grounded
+    sentences because `{'-1.07'} != {'−1.07'}` byte-wise. This
+    normalization closes that mismatch."""
+    if not text:
+        return text
+    return (
+        text.replace("−", "-")  # U+2212 MINUS SIGN
+            .replace("–", "-")  # U+2013 EN DASH
+            .replace("—", "-")  # U+2014 EM DASH
+            .replace("‒", "-")  # U+2012 FIGURE DASH
+    )
+
+
 def _numbers_in(text: str) -> set[str]:
-    return {m.group(0) for m in _NUMBER_RE.finditer(text or "")}
+    text = _normalize_unicode_minus(text or "")
+    return {m.group(0) for m in _NUMBER_RE.finditer(text)}

+    text = _normalize_unicode_minus(text or "")
+    return {m.group(0) for m in _DECIMAL_NUMBER_RE.finditer(text)}

verdict: REQUEST_CHANGES
diagnosis_correct: PARTIAL
with_evidence: |
  I could not read the requested current-path evidence files because outputs/honest_sweep_r3/clinical/clinical_tirzepatide_t2dm currently has no evidence_pool.json or verification_details.json and has a zero-byte reasoning_trace.jsonl. I read the preserved run at outputs/honest_sweep_r3.before_verifier_fix/clinical/clinical_tirzepatide_t2dm plus outputs/v4_reasoning_traces/efficacy_regen.txt.
  The unicode-minus diagnosis is real: verification_details.json lines 15-17 drop the ev_001 meta-analysis sentence for 1.07/1.44/0.56/11.36/4.62, and the evidence contains those values with mixed U+002D/U+2212 signs.
  The span-narrow diagnosis is also real: efficacy_regen.txt lines 31-38 show V4 Pro identifying ev_017 SURPASS table values, while verification_details.json lines 89-92/108-112/143-147 show 0-500 spans on ev_017/ev_021 missing later table values.
  But the diagnosis is not TRUE globally. Example: verification_details.json lines 89-92 includes SURPASS-3 "-2.20"; I searched ev_017/ev_021 and did not find 2.20 as an outcome value. Some drops are still real unsupported synthesis, not verifier-only false positives.

holes_in_fix:
  - p0_or_p1_finding: |
      P1: Full-direct_quote fallback is too permissive. provenance_generator.py lines 719-753 accepts a sentence if all missing decimals appear anywhere in the cited evidence's full direct_quote. That can validate a claim assembled from unrelated parts of a 25k-char review/page. Your cancer 50% example is a real failure mode if the narrow span shares two content words and the full document contains "50%" elsewhere. Entailment helps only in enforce mode and is now asked to judge huge mixed-context evidence.
  - p0_or_p1_finding: |
      P1: The fix patches verifier acceptance instead of repairing the actual span source. live_deepseek_generator.py lines 244-322 still emits (0, 500) when no single 500-char window contains every sentence decimal. Many bad spans are produced by the span rewriter after the model emits [ev_XXX], not by V4 Pro choosing byte ranges. Safer fix: recover one or more local support windows and verify those, not whole-document pass-through.
  - p0_or_p1_finding: |
      P1: Content-word grounding remains narrow-span-only. provenance_generator.py lines 786-795 still checks only aggregated_span_text. After your numeric fallback, grounded table sentences can still fail no_content_word_overlap because the span is 0-500 while support is later. I reproduced this for Efficacy SURPASS-4, SURPASS-5, SURPASS-6, and SURMOUNT-2 examples.
  - p0_or_p1_finding: |
      P1: Trial-name strictness is still generating known false negatives, including primary evidence. ev_000/ev_018 are SURPASS-2 primary papers, but title/statement/direct_quote as stored do not contain "SURPASS-2", so provenance_generator.py lines 599-620 and 802-815 reject valid SURPASS-2 sentences. This needs metadata/alias repair, not full direct_quote scanning.
  - p0_or_p1_finding: |
      P1: Integer-only fallback is unsafe. provenance_generator.py lines 764-777 passes if any integer overlaps the full evidence. For integer-heavy clinical framing, one coincidental N/week/year/dose can validate otherwise unsupported integer claims.

predicted_residual_failures: |
  1. Efficacy SURPASS-4 sentence at verification_details.json lines 108-112: numeric fallback removes the number miss, but no_content_word_overlap_any_cited_span and trial_name_mismatch remain.
  2. Efficacy SURPASS-6 sentence at lines 143-147: numbers are in ev_017 full text, but content overlap and trial-name mismatch remain.
  3. Efficacy SURMOUNT-2 report sentence at lines 276-280: ev_002/ev_020 full text contains the HbA1c numbers, but content overlap and trial-name mismatch remain.
  4. Safety SURPASS-2 adverse-event sentence at lines 413-416: numeric fallback should pass the AE percentages, but SURPASS-2 trial_name_mismatch remains.

other_verifier_bugs_to_investigate:
  - provenance_generator.py:473-488: unicode list covers observed U+2212/U+2013/U+2014 in this pool, but not general variants such as U+2010, U+2011, U+2015, U+FE58, U+FE63, U+FF0D, U+207B, U+208B. Also do not blindly map range dashes to minus; "8.12-8.21" becomes a fake negative second endpoint.
  - evidence_pool unicode scan: observed U+2219 BULLET OPERATOR in ev_021 as decimal separator ("-1∙91"). _DECIMAL_NUMBER_RE will not match this against model output "-1.91".
  - _NUMBER_RE/_DECIMAL_NUMBER_RE: thousands separators are mishandled; "1,879" becomes "1" and "879", not "1879".
  - _PLACEBO_COMPARATOR_RE/_THRESHOLD_RE: normalization is not applied before these regexes; ≤ thresholds are not stripped, and integer thresholds can leak into the weak integer branch.
  - _content_words: ASCII-only tokenization drops or mangles β-cells, nonbreaking-hyphen GLP‑1, and other biomedical unicode tokens.

trial_name_middle_ground_proposal: REFINE
rationale: |
  Do not allow trial names by scanning full direct_quote plus matching numbers. That recreates the old review-paper context leak.
  Middle ground: allow a trial name from direct_quote only when it appears in the cited span or in a repaired local support window that also contains the sentence's claim numbers/comparator terms. If a primary paper for that trial exists in the evidence pool, require that primary evidence be co-cited or carry an explicit metadata alias. For ev_000/ev_018, add an authoritative trial_aliases field mapping the NEJM paper to SURPASS-2.

additional_investigations_i_should_have_done:
  - Re-run the full smoke before/after and diff drop reasons, not one sentence.
  - Count how many spans are still 0-500 fallbacks after the fix.
  - For every full-evidence pass, locate minimal local windows proving all numbers/content/trial names co-occur.
  - Add adversarial tests where the full document contains the right number in an unrelated context.
  - Run a unicode numeric census across all evidence pools, not only tirzepatide.
  - Test enforce/warn/off entailment modes separately; the mechanical verifier should remain safe with the judge disabled.
  - Add unit tests for U+2219 decimals, en-dash ranges, thousands commas, ≤ thresholds, and integer-only fabricated framing.

convergence_call: continue
